   $(document).ready(function() {
        	$("#udm").menu({ position: { using: setSubMenu } }); 
            $("#udm > li > a > span.ui-icon-caret-1-e").after("<span class='udmA' style='display: block; margin-top: 7px; clip: rect(0px 8px 8px 0px); visibility: visible;'><img src='/wps/themes/html/ACSDefault/images/menu_arrow1.gif' alt='menu' title=''></span>");
    		$("#udm > li > a > span.ui-icon-caret-1-e").remove();	
    		$("#udm > li > ul > li > a > span.ui-icon-caret-1-e").removeClass("ui-icon-caret-1-e").addClass("ui-icon-triangle-1-e");

			function setSubMenu(position, elements) { 
				var options = { 
				  of: elements.target.element 
				}; 
		 		if (elements.element.element.parent().parent().attr("id") === "udm") { 
					options.my = "left top"; 
					options.at = "left bottom"; 
				} else { 
					options.my = "left top"; 
					var listItemCount = 0;
					$(this).find("li").each(function(index,value){
						listItemCount++;
					});
					if(listItemCount > 15)
						if(document.all)
							options.at = "right top-80";
						else
							options.at = "right top-110"; 
					else 
						options.at = "right top";
				} 
				elements.element.element.position(options); 
			}; 
		var initialLeftValue = 400 + $(this).scrollLeft();
		var initialTopValue = 250 +  $(this).scrollTop();
		$('#floatlayer').css('top', initialTopValue + "px");
		$('#floatlayer').css('left', initialLeftValue + "px");
		if (window.pageXOffset == undefined){
			$(window).scroll(function(){
				var scrollLeftValue = 400 + (document.documentElement.scrollLeft ? document.documentElement.scrollLeft : document.body.scrollLeft);			
				var scrollTopValue = 250 + (document.documentElement.scrollTop ? document.documentElement.scrollTop : document.body.scrollTop);
				$('#floatlayer').css('top', scrollTopValue + "px");
				$('#floatlayer').css('left', scrollLeftValue + "px");
			});
		}
		});
  </script>

               <script>
                function printPage(id) {

			if (document.getElementById != null) {

				var html = '<html>';
				html += '\n<head>';
				if (document.getElementByTagName != null) {

					if (document.getElementByTagName("head").length > 0) 

						html += document.getElementByTagName("head")[0].innerHTML;
					

				}
				// Added hideCalendarImg() as part of the defect #ESPRD00803676 to hide the calendar image in the print window
				html += '\n</head>';
				html += '\n <body onload=printWin.focus();printWin.print();printWin.close();disableLinks();hideCalendarImg();disableButtons();disableControls();enableButtons();>\n';
				var printReadyElem = document.getElementById(id);

				if (printReadyElem != null) {

					html += printReadyElem.innerHTML;

				}

				else {

					return;

				}

				html += '\n<BR><form><input type="button" class="actions" value="Print" onClick="window.print();">&nbsp;&nbsp;<input type="button" class="actions" value="Close" onClick="window.close();"></form>';
				html += "</body>";
				html += "</html>";
				var printWin = window
						.open(
								"",
								"printPage",
								"resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes,menubar=no,toolbar=no,status=no,width=1000,height=500,screenX=100,screenY=100,top=100,left=100");
				//ENDS HERE

				if (document.all) {
					printWin.document.open();
					printWin.document.write(html);
					printWin.document.close();
					
				} else {
					printWin.document.open();
					printWin.document.write(html);
					printWin.document.close();
					
				}
			} else {
				alert("The print ready feature is only available if you are using an browser. Please update your browser.");
			}
		}
               </script>

                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <b>
                       Division of Public Assistance Announces Office Consolidation
                      </b>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <b>
                       <br/>
                      </b>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      Effective March 1, 2021, the Anchorage Offices of the Division of Public Assistance moved on March 1, 2021 to the University Center Mall, 3901 Old Seward Highway, Suite 131, Anchorage, AK 99503. For more information, visit
                      <a href="http://dhss.alaska.gov/dpa/Documents/dpa/press/DPA-Office-Moves.pdf">
                       Consolidation of DPA Anchorage Offices
                      </a>
                      .
                      <b>
                       <br/>
                      </b>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <b>
                       <br/>
                      </b>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <b>
                       <br/>
                      </b>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <b>
                       COVID-19 Vaccine Now Available to All Alaskans Age 16 and Older
                      </b>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <br/>
                      On 03/09/2021, Alaska Governor Mike Dunleavy
                      <a href="https://gov.alaska.gov/newsroom/2021/03/09/dunleavy-announces-covid-19-vaccine-available-to-all-alaskans/">
                       announced
                      </a>
                      the COVID-19 vaccine is available for all individuals who live or work in Alaska and are age 16 and older, making Alaska the first state in the nation to remove eligibility requirements. Visit
                      <a href="http://dhss.alaska.gov/dph/Epi/id/Pages/COVID-19/Vaccineappointments.aspx">
                       covidvax.alaska.gov
                      </a>
                      or call 907.646.3322 for more information and to sign up for a COVID-19 vaccination.
                      <b>
                       <br/>
                      </b>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <b>
                       <br/>
                      </b>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <b>
                       <br/>
                      </b>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <b>
                       State of Alaska’s Declaration of Public Health Disaster Emergency Expired 02/14/2021
                      </b>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <b>
                       <br/>
                      </b>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      As of February 14, 2021, the State of Alaska’s Declaration of Public Health Disaster Emergency (DD), which was in place to manage its response to COVID-19, expired. While certain authorities under the DD have expired, the Department of Health and Social Services (DHSS) is making every effort to minimize potential disruption to interactions between Alaskans and DHSS as we transition out of the DD.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      Accordingly, until further instructed by the Governor or the Alaska Legislature:
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <br/>
                     </p>
                     <ul>
                      <li>
                       DHSS will continue to operate its COVID-19 response under the same guidance and direction that had previously been provided, which includes all prior waived or suspended statutes and regulations.
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       DHSS will continue to manage its Medicaid program under the federal authorities outlined in the federal blanket waivers, the 1135 Waiver, and the Appendix K approvals, since those authorities are tied to the federal public health emergency and are not dependent on a state declaration.
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       DHSS will continue to work with our federal partners to ensure a smooth transition for vaccinations, therapeutics, and other critical services that DHSS had been managing under the Declaration.
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       All mitigation efforts for the health and safety of state employees will remain in effect.
                      </li>
                     </ul>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <br/>
                      The end of this disaster declaration does not mean the virus is gone and we can stop taking measures to keep ourselves and others healthy and safe. DHSS' primary concern remains the health and safety of all Alaskans, and we will continue to consider that paramount concern in our decisions as we navigate the next phase of the state’s response to COVID-19.
                      <b>
                       <br/>
                      </b>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <b>
                       <br/>
                      </b>
                     </p>
                     <br/>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <b>
                       CMS Extension of Indian Health Service and Tribal Facilities “Four Walls” Requirement
                      </b>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <br/>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      On January 15, 2021, the Centers for Medicare and Medicaid Services (CMS) announced an
                      <a href="https://www.medicaid.gov/federal-policy-guidance/downloads/cib11421.pdf">
                       Extension of Grace Period Related to the “Four Walls” Requirement under 42 C.F.R. § 440.90 for Indian Health Service and Tribal Facilities
                      </a>
                      . As a result, Medicaid reimbursement for covered services provided outside the clinic by IHS/Tribal health providers will continue through October 31, 2021. The Department of Health and Social Services will continue to work with IHS/Tribal health providers to develop a plan to address coverage of these services after the expiration of this extension.
                     </p>
                     <div>
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div>
                      <br/>
                     </div>

                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <strong>
                       Alaska Responders Relief Line – 844.985.8275
                      </strong>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <strong>
                      </strong>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      <strong>
                       <br/>
                      </strong>
                     </p>
                     <p style="margin: 0px;">
                      Recognizing the unique stressors that providers face, the Division of Behavioral Health has established a 24/7 support line, 844.985.8275, for healthcare and behavioral professionals impacted by COVID personally and professionally. Staff supporting the call line recognize callers are often first responders and will allows callers to openly express their experiences and feelings serving Alaskans impacted by COVID. This service is also available to immediate family members of first responders who may be experiencing stress, anxiety and other hard to label emotions as a result of their loved one engaging on the front lines.
                     </p>

                function printPage(id) {

			if (document.getElementById != null) {

				var html = '<html>';
				html += '\n<head>';
				if (document.getElementByTagName != null) {

					if (document.getElementByTagName("head").length > 0) 

						html += document.getElementByTagName("head")[0].innerHTML;
					

				}
				// Added hideCalendarImg() as part of the defect #ESPRD00803676 to hide the calendar image in the print window
				html += '\n</head>';
				html += '\n <body onload=printWin.focus();printWin.print();printWin.close();disableLinks();hideCalendarImg();disableButtons();disableControls();enableButtons();>\n';
				var printReadyElem = document.getElementById(id);

				if (printReadyElem != null) {

					html += printReadyElem.innerHTML;

				}

				else {

					return;

				}

				html += '\n<BR><form><input type="button" class="actions" value="Print" onClick="window.print();">&nbsp;&nbsp;<input type="button" class="actions" value="Close" onClick="window.close();"></form>';
				html += "</body>";
				html += "</html>";
				var printWin = window
						.open(
								"",
								"printPage",
								"resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes,menubar=no,toolbar=no,status=no,width=1000,height=500,screenX=100,screenY=100,top=100,left=100");
				//ENDS HERE

				if (document.all) {
					printWin.document.open();
					printWin.document.write(html);
					printWin.document.close();
					
				} else {
					printWin.document.open();
					printWin.document.write(html);
					printWin.document.close();
					
				}
			} else {
				alert("The print ready feature is only available if you are using an browser. Please update your browser.");
			}
		}

                function printPage(id) {

			if (document.getElementById != null) {

				var html = '<html>';
				html += '\n<head>';
				if (document.getElementByTagName != null) {

					if (document.getElementByTagName("head").length > 0) 

						html += document.getElementByTagName("head")[0].innerHTML;
					

				}
				// Added hideCalendarImg() as part of the defect #ESPRD00803676 to hide the calendar image in the print window
				html += '\n</head>';
				html += '\n <body onload=printWin.focus();printWin.print();printWin.close();disableLinks();hideCalendarImg();disableButtons();disableControls();enableButtons();>\n';
				var printReadyElem = document.getElementById(id);

				if (printReadyElem != null) {

					html += printReadyElem.innerHTML;

				}

				else {

					return;

				}

				html += '\n<BR><form><input type="button" class="actions" value="Print" onClick="window.print();">&nbsp;&nbsp;<input type="button" class="actions" value="Close" onClick="window.close();"></form>';
				html += "</body>";
				html += "</html>";
				var printWin = window
						.open(
								"",
								"printPage",
								"resizable=yes,scrollbars=yes,menubar=no,toolbar=no,status=no,width=1000,height=500,screenX=100,screenY=100,top=100,left=100");
				//ENDS HERE

				if (document.all) {
					printWin.document.open();
					printWin.document.write(html);
					printWin.document.close();
					
				} else {
					printWin.document.open();
					printWin.document.write(html);
					printWin.document.close();
					
				}
			} else {
				alert("The print ready feature is only available if you are using an browser. Please update your browser.");
			}
		}
